Datensatzgruppenabfrage                    : Select bill_no    ,
       bill_date  ,
       bill_time  ,
       bill_amt,       
       Ad_Date,
       AD_U_ID    ,
       MACHINE_NO,
       pr_rep
 From 
(
Select bill_no    ,
       bill_date  ,
       bill_time  ,
       Round(bill_amt+nvl(vat_amt,0)-Nvl(Disc_amt,0),:Parameter.No_Of_Decimal) bill_amt   ,
       Ad_Date    ,
       AD_U_ID    ,
       MACHINE_NO,
       pr_rep
From ias_pos_hst_bill_mst 
Where machine_no = :Parameter.machine_no
  And Nvl(hung,0)= 0
  And To_Date(Bill_Date,'DD/MM/YYYY')>=decode (:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date,null,To_Date(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_CurDate,'DD/MM/YYYY'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date)-Nvl(:Parameter.Num_of_days_shw_bills,1)
and ( :Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists (Select 1 From User_R Where U_Id=ias_pos_hst_bill_mst.ad_u_id
                 Connect By Prior U_Id = U_Mng Start With U_Id = :Parameter.User_No) )
Union  
Select bill_no    ,
       bill_date  ,
       bill_time  ,
       Round(bill_amt+nvl(vat_amt,0)-Nvl(Disc_amt,0),:Parameter.No_Of_Decimal) bill_amt   ,
       Ad_Date    ,
       AD_U_ID    ,
       MACHINE_NO ,
       pr_rep
From ias_pos_bill_mst 
Where To_Date(Bill_Date,'DD/MM/YYYY')>=decode (:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date,null,To_Date(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_CurDate,'DD/MM/YYYY'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date)-Nvl(:Parameter.Num_of_days_shw_bills,1)
and ( :Parameter.User_No=1 or Exists (Select 1 From User_R Where U_Id=ias_pos_bill_mst.ad_u_id
                 Connect By Prior U_Id = U_Mng Start With U_Id = :Parameter.User_No) )
  And Nvl(hung,0)= 0
) 
 Order By Ad_Date  Desc
